        ( [ $A $B ])) $T)) 
            ( (M --> 
                ( [ $A ])) 
                    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$A','$B']]]],T]],[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$B']]]],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( (M --> 
        ( [ $A $B ])) $T)) 
            ( (M --> 
                ( [ $B ])) 
                    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

  (|- 
    ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T)) 
  ( ($S --> $M) 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

  (|- 
    ( ($M --> 
        ($S & $P)) $T)) 
  ( ($M --> $S) 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[!,A],T]],[A,['Truth_Negation',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( (! $A) $T)) 
  ($A 
    (Truth_Negation $T)))

    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))

  ( ($B && $A) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[A,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])

    ( ($B ==> $C) $T2))

    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[A,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|-

    ( ($A ==> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> $B)

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(=

  ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,&&,B]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==> 
      ($A && $B)) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,'||',B]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])

    ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($C ==>
